Func DUONGCAOTOC()
	If Not $g_bComboSent Then
		_SendComboOnce()
	EndIf
	GUICtrlSetData($CRACK, "25")
_DUONGCAOTOC()  ;Checkpoint 2
	Local $start = TimerInit()
	While TimerDiff($start) < 1
		_MEMORYPOINTERWRITE($FINALADDRESS, $HMEMORY, $OFFSET1, "3218789416")
		_MEMORYPOINTERWRITE($FINALADDRESS, $HMEMORY, $OFFSET2, "3228005313")
		_MEMORYPOINTERWRITE($FINALADDRESS, $HMEMORY, $OFFSET3, "1077885796")
	WEnd

_DUONGCAOTOC()  ;Checkpoint 3
_MEMORYPOINTERWRITE($FINALADDRESS, $HMEMORY, $OFFSET1, "1071575550")
